# Firefox CSS calc() Value Overflow

## Your Task

Firefox crashes when processing CSS calc() with extreme values. Find the C++ source files in mozilla/gecko-dev that (1) parse CSS calc() expressions and (2) handle numeric overflow during calc() value resolution.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the incident domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/firefox--871325b8.

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## CSS calc() in Firefox — Key Files

### Parsing (1)
- **`servo/components/style/values/specified/calc.rs`** — The main Rust parser for CSS `calc()` and related math functions (`min()`, `max()`, `clamp()`, `round()`, `sin()`, etc.). Defines the `MathFunction` enum, `Leaf` node types, and `CalcLengthPercentage`.
- **`servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs`** — Generic calc AST (`GenericCalcNode`) with parsing helpers and the `simplify_and_sort` implementation per CSS Values 4 spec.

### Overflow Handling (2)
The overflow protection forms a chain from Rust → C++ bridge → C++:

1. **`servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs`** (`resolve_internal`) — Handles IEEE 754 infinity/NaN in the Rust evaluation layer
2. **`servo/components/style/values/computed/length_percentage.rs`** (`resolve`) — Applies `clamping_mode` (NonNegative, etc.) after resolution
3. **`servo/ports/geckolib/glue.rs`** (`Servo_ResolveCalcLengthPercentage`) — C-callable bridge returning the resolved `f32`
4. **`layout/style/ServoStyleConstsInlines.h`** (`StyleCalcLengthPercentage::Resolve`, `DefaultPercentLengthToAppUnits`) — Converts CSS pixels to `nscoord` using clamped functions
5. **`gfx/src/nsCoord.h`** (`NSToCoordRoundWithClamp`, `NSToCoordTruncClamped`) — The key overflow protection: bounds-checks float values against `nscoord_MAX`/`nscoord_MIN` before converting to `int32_t`
